    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_175013378" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/175013378" />
    <a title="Sylvia " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4557869-sylvia"><img alt="Sylvia " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1432475002p2/4557869.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/175013378?book_show_action=true">Jun 08, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sylvia " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sylvia " href="/user/show/4557869-sylvia">Sylvia </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780330529747" href="/book/show/13041606-dreamless">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4557869-sylvia?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4557869-sylvia?shelf=bad-boys-for-the-red-room">bad-boys-for-the-red-room</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4557869-sylvia?shelf=male-pov">male-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4557869-sylvia?shelf=all-time-favourite-ya">all-time-favourite-ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4557869-sylvia?shelf=greek-mythology">greek-mythology</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4557869-sylvia?shelf=dual-multiple-pov">dual-multiple-pov</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer175013378" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7642951522008909749">Oh my word I did not want this book to end. What can I say the Gods must be doing something right by giving Josephine Angelini a remarkable ability to spin a web of adventure rooted deep in mythology and tragedy. This book was an amazing follow up to Starcrossed, which I adored but had me screaming and yelling at the end in disbelief. We left off with the notion that Lucas and Helen were actually related and that the love they share and have for one another is forbidden. But we know the stinking</span>
  <span id="freeText7642951522008909749" style="display:none">Oh my word I did not want this book to end. What can I say the Gods must be doing something right by giving Josephine Angelini a remarkable ability to spin a web of adventure rooted deep in mythology and tragedy. This book was an amazing follow up to Starcrossed, which I adored but had me screaming and yelling at the end in disbelief. We left off with the notion that Lucas and Helen were actually related and that the love they share and have for one another is forbidden. But we know the stinking truth and it's the only thing we have to go on when picking up Dreamless. You don't know how desperate I was to find this book. The mere anticipation was boiling over and as soon as I got my hands on this baby I never let it go. <br /><br />I was mesmerised, captivated and enthralled at the get go. I was completely enamoured with the story and how dark and gothic like it had become. I was completely intrigued by the major role that Helen played in this and found her to be matured, selfless, heroic and one bad ass demigod. She is the Descender and the only one who can enter the Underworld to try and break the curse by killing the Furies. This curse keeps family members apart from one another all for the sake of a blood oath. It's a humongous burden that Helen bears, wandering the Underworld and trying to forget the one boy she is forbidden to be with, Lucas! Oh dear lord in heaven. Why must we endure the torture of these two being apart? But worse still, why must they be tormented for even looking at each other? Seriously my heart breaks every time I think of the pain they go through by just speaking each other's name. But the pain was more unbearable when told from Lucas's POV. The tragedy and beauty that deems this relationship makes me want to quote Shakespeare it's that crazy insane. What's worse is we know the truth dammit and watch them suffer through it, well more Lucas. He's love for her is so unwavering and selfless to the point that he would even encourage the new guy, Mr Adonis himself Orion, to woo her (well so to speak). <br /><br />Orion, who is an outcast, has been sent by Daphne (don't make me swear when I say her name she makes me so mad. She is selfish!) to the Underworld too. He is a descendant of Adonis and can seduce and control desire. Now the notion of a love triangle infuriated me. I was not liking it one bit. How can Helen even think about looking at anyone else but Lucas. WE KNOW the truth about them so why add another guy to the mix? Because it keeps us guessing and wanting more and I have to say I really liked Orion. He didn't push or intrude if that makes sense. He's relationship with Helen actually felt natural. Don't get me wrong I am all for Lucas (he has my heart) and Helen, but it's really hard to explain unless you read it. Once you do you will understand the importance of Orion's role in the story, and to Helen and Lucas as well. <br /><br />So much goes down in the story and I'm not going to reveal any of it. You all just have to read it for yourselves. All I'm going to say is that I was so frustrated by the torment and torture that Helen and Lucas endured *bangs fist against wall imagining Daphne's head* This is all her fault. And right to the end she continued to keep the truth away from them. They still don't know arrrggghhhh!! I think she is up to no good and has something big up her sleeve. At one point I really wanted to slap her and wished the Furies set Helen on her own mother. I would have loved to see Daphne fry. I know, I know it's a bad thing to say but I loathe that woman. Right till the EPIC end she wanted Helen to do more even though at that point she'd done enough. So annoying. Anyways, the end was magnificent and again we are left with a cliffhanger leaving us wanting more. I eagerly await book 3 and am going to suffer terribly in the meantime. <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7642951522008909749" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_195937937" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/195937937" />
    <a title="Maria " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5769334-maria"><img alt="Maria " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1600318539p2/5769334.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/195937937?book_show_action=true">Aug 07, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maria " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maria " href="/user/show/5769334-maria">Maria </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer195937937" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6336212238114430349"><b>MY REACTION AFTER READING THE BOOK:</b><br/><br/><a href='http://media.photobucket.com/image/sad%20gifs/torzatheexplorer/gifs/sad.gif?o=38' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380356270ra/707981.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><a href='http://media.photobucket.com/image/depressed%20gif/roseofsharon33/GIF%20Response/depression.gif?o=14' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380356270ra/707982.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>It's not crying because it's not entirely bad. I am not saying it's bad, its just thatI didn't enjoy this as much as I enjoyed the first book.<br/><br/>Read further to know why.<br/><br/><br/><b>THE GIST</b><br/><br/>Starcrossed ended with a huge <s>frustrating</s> cliffhanger! Turns out Helen and Lucas were cousins <s>imagine that?!</s> <br/><br/><s>AfsdhgjuntwpetfpnCGTPNEGUSDBFVHAVGNOYAWERY</s><br/><br/>Okay going back, Helen is a Descender meaning she is could go down to the Underworld eventhough she isn't dead yet. Why does she ha</span>
  <span id="freeText6336212238114430349" style="display:none"><b>MY REACTION AFTER READING THE BOOK:</b><br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/sad%20gifs/torzatheexplorer/gifs/sad.gif?o=38" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380356270ra/707981.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/depressed%20gif/roseofsharon33/GIF%20Response/depression.gif?o=14" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380356270ra/707982.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>It's not crying because it's not entirely bad. I am not saying it's bad, its just thatI didn't enjoy this as much as I enjoyed the first book.<br><br>Read further to know why.<br><br><br><b>THE GIST</b><br><br>Starcrossed ended with a huge <s>frustrating</s> cliffhanger! Turns out Helen and Lucas were cousins <s>imagine that?!</s> <br><br><s>AfsdhgjuntwpetfpnCGTPNEGUSDBFVHAVGNOYAWERY</s><br><br>Okay going back, Helen is a Descender meaning she is could go down to the Underworld eventhough she isn't dead yet. Why does she have to go down to there? She needs to break the curse of the Furies. It's a very big responsibility for her. To make matters worse, she was forbidden to be with the guy she loves, Lucas(WTH right?!).<br><br>To make matters even more complicated, enter Orion (the first Scion) and a Descender as well sent by Daphne (Helen's selfish mother) to help Helen on her task.<br><br>Will Helen and Lucas find out the truth about them?<br>Will Helen be successful killing the Furies and stop the blood feud?<br>What is Orion's role in all of this? <br>What is Helen's mother (that sly woman!) up to?<br><br><br><b>FIRST IMPRESSION</b><br><br>Of course, Starcrossed was one of the first books I've read after I switched from reading mystery novels. It's one of the YA books I've read that really amazed me. I was an immediate fan and after the first book I obviously wanted to get my hands on the second one.<br><br>I so wanted to get my hands on Dreamless because I was so sure that it would be as good as or much better than the first one.<br><br>So here is my initial reaction:<br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/excited%20gif/princessaili/gif%20macros/tumblr_m61icbmLdC1rnesb2.gif?o=33" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380356270ra/707983.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/excited%20gif/sporker05/gif/yay.gif?o=46" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380356270ra/707984.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><b>CHARACTERS</b><br><br>Lets start with Helen. I've always loved Helen in Starcrossed. Not much of a fan of her here. On the first book she was this real pretty girl with awesome powers plus she wasn't the typical whiny girl who needs to be saved a lot. Imagine my surprise when that all changed in Dreamless. She was the exact type of female lead I hated in books! Gosh if I had those powers girl I would have been kickass and fearless! I wouldn't need a guy to save my ass at all! There wasn't much to like about Helen on this book aside from the fact that she is doing what she is tasked to do without complaint and I think that is admirable. She gets better as the book goes but still she was still a "damsel in distress" for me in this book.<br><br>I was extremely disappointed in Lucas. I get that he's in pain that they couldn't be together but give me a break! I mean he could have done research on the problem that they were having or really verify if they were really cousins. I mean people lie and well Helen's mother did. It was up to them to prove her wrong if he was really thinking! But no he wasn't. He thought that making Helen hate him was a good plan or avoiding her or pushing her to Orion. I mean come on Lucas! You are one of my favorites and don't let me down on the third book please! He was also MIA in this book a lot so don't expect to see much of him.<br><br>The first Scion Orion was a breath of fresh air. I mean having a love triangle isn't but with the tension in this book I think it was only right that Orion was added. At first I thought I'd get mad at him but then he proves to be one good character. He's good looking, funny and among other things he cared for Helen at the time she needed someone's support the most. <br><br>I hated Helen's mother to the CORE!<br><br>The other characters doesn't seem to care much about Helen on this book. Its a good thing Orion was there for her.<br><br><br><b>LUCAS + HELEN = TOTALLY DEPRESSING</b><br><br>I want to pull all of my hair out because of how frustrated I was in what happened to them. I loved their relationship in Starcrossed and was totally depressed in Dreamless. The whole "cousin" thing really got me thinking a lot about Filipino soap opera! This is the kind of stuff that I thought you could only get at a Filipino drama series. Turns out I was wrong.<br><br><b>ORION + HELEN = UNEXPECTED</b><br><br>It was fun reading about them. I mean it was kind of innocent for me which is what I liked. Orion was a good guy (at least for now I think). Orion and Helen had chemistry too which was good. And I liked him for sticking around for Helen. Kudos to you ORION!<br><br><br><b>QUOTABLE QUOTES</b><br><br><i>“Even if it kills me, staying awake and seeing you... is better than any dream.”</i><br><br><i>“It's not our talents that make us safe or dangerous, it's our choices.” </i><br><br><i>“You're my invisible sun, aren't you?”</i><br><br><br><b>HIGHLIGHTS</b><br><br>- ORION was the most important highlight for me in this book.<br><br>- The mythology was still as good as the first one.<br><br><br><b>FINAL WORDS </b><br><br>I am a fan of this series and still am but I am just not happy with how things turned out after the second book. I am a huge fan of Ms. Angelini because he writing style is definitely something that I adore. <br><br>There were a lot of parts in this book that shouldn't have been there anymore in my opinion. It was so overloaded with stuff that was not necessary. There were tons of new information and before I could process them all new information would be given. I don't know if I am just really slow or there really is a problem with it because as far as the ratings go this book is getting high ones.<br><br>There was something missing in this book that apparently was present in the previous one. I just couldn't put my finger on what it is but maybe it was because there was so littl of Helen and Lucas moments I don't really know. <br><br>I am getting entirely upset on the Lucas-Helen are cousins drama. I hate the fact that no one seemed to want to find out if Daphne was telling the truth even Lucas and Helen didn't seem to want to disprove Daphne's claim because no one was trying to figure out if its true or not. It's upsetting. Drama like this is the reason why I don't often watch Filipino drama because things like this ALWAYS happen.<br><br>I am disappointed. Very actually. But this series for me is still worth finishing. I am definitely looking forward to seeing Helen and Lucas happy and together!<br><br><b>3 stars</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="6336212238114430349" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('/aFKez3iR7sFOiQiyGlghZNKbSNNr9GmlMdCt/0yJB3yZ4DzE3WiViAvU6K4xj3tZql1HzDexc9AE5VJHmPYLg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('n7r+8ga5x253Vuj+ej3+HVDR3Gskywn92qaI5OBuEniQfDR6KC4ig1JDn34KkqN1pTLEV1m6HZQOcl8aAz/uSw==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer16300054249168438465">Josephine Angelini is a Massachusetts native and the youngest of eight siblings. She graduated from New York University's Tisch School of the Arts in theater, with a focus on the classics. She now lives in Los Angeles with her husband and daughter.</span>
